
The parity check matrix for W(3,31) minus a spread is a 32b x 
31b matrix, where b is 962.

The 1 coordinates of the first row of the circulants in the (q+1)xq rep matrix is \
given by Hrep.

The length of the code is 29822 and the check matrix has rank 
15873, so the full code has dimension 13949.

There is a generator matrix for the subcode of the form (P | id) where P is quasi \
cyclic 14b x 17b matrix, whose first rows are in the matrix Pbin.

The subcode has dimension 13468 so the rate is 0.4516129032258064.
